ton	1 Ko e fono ki he kau tamaioʻeiki. 5 Ki he tamaioʻeiki kuo tui

ton	ʻaofi ʻaki ia ʻae koula, ke haʻamo ʻaki ʻae palepale.
ton	Ke ua hono hokoʻanga ʻi he laupapa pe taha, ke tuʻu hangatonu
ton	atu pe ʻae taha ki he taha: pea ke fai pehē pe ki he laupapa
ton	kotoa pē ʻoe fale fehikitaki.
ton	¶ “Pea te ke ngaohi ʻae lotoʻā ʻoe fale fehikitaki: ki he
ton	potu ʻoku hanga ki tonga ʻe ai ʻae ngaahi puipui tautau ʻoe
ton	tupenu tuʻovalevale, ko e hanga ʻe uangeau hono lōloa ki he

ton	fā: ko hono ʻuluaki ʻotu ko e satio, mo e topasi, mo e
ton	kapukeli: ko hono ʻuluaki ʻotu ia.
ton	Pea te ke ʻai ia ki he kato pe taha, pea ʻomi ia ʻi he kato,
ton	fakataha mo e pulu mo e sipitangata ʻe ua.

ton	ʻae fakalelei, ke fakanofo mo fakatapui ʻakinautolu: ka ʻe
ton	ʻikai kai ia ʻe ha tokotaha kehe, he ʻoku tapu ia.
ton	Pea te ke toʻo ʻae ngaahi paʻanga fakalelei ʻae fānau ʻa
ton	ʻIsileli, ʻo vahe ia ki he ngāue ʻoe fale fakatahaʻanga
ton	ʻoe kakai: koeʻuhi ke hoko ia ko e meʻa fakamanatu ki he
ton	fānau ʻa ʻIsileli ʻi he ʻao ʻo Sihova, ke fai ʻaki ʻae
ton	fakalelei ki homou laumālie.”
ton	Ko e fale fakatahaʻanga ʻoe kakai, mo e puha ʻoe fuakava, mo
ton	e nofoʻanga ʻaloʻofa ʻoku hilifaki ki hono funga, mo hono
ton	ngaahi nāunau kotoa pē ʻoe fale fehikitaki,

ton	ʻoku mavava ʻi he mālohi, pea ʻoku ʻikai ko e leʻo
ton	ʻonautolu ʻoku tangi ʻi he fakavaivaiʻi: ka ʻoku ou ongoʻi
ton	ʻae leʻo ʻonautolu ʻoku hiva.”
ton	¶ Pea naʻe pehē ʻe Mōsese kia Sihova, “Vakai, ʻoku ke

ton	mo au. Ka kuo ke tala mai, ʻOku ou ʻilo koe ʻi ho hingoa, pea
ton	kuo ʻofeina koe ʻi hoku ʻao.
ton	¶ “Pea te ke tauhi ʻae kātoanga ʻoe mā taʻefakalēvani.
ton	Ke ke kai ʻae mā taʻefakalēvani ʻi he ʻaho ʻe fitu, ʻo
ton	hangē ko ʻeku fekau kiate koe, ʻi he ngaahi ʻaho ʻoe

ton	ua, ke velo ai ʻae ongo ʻakau ke haʻamo ʻaki.

ton	kuo hoko ʻae kau Filisitia kiate koe.” Pea naʻe motumotuhi
ton	ʻe ia ʻae ngaahi afo, ʻo hangē ko e motu ha foʻi filo
ton	vaivai ʻoka lave ki ai ʻae afi. Pea ko ia naʻe ʻikai ʻilo
ton	¶ Pea naʻe ai ʻae tangata talavou ʻe taha mei Petelihema
ton	Siuta ʻi he faʻahinga ʻo Siuta, ko e Livai ia, pea naʻe nofo
ton	Pea naʻa nau tangi ki he fānau ʻa Tani. Pea naʻa nau tangaki
ton	kimui, ʻo pehē kia Maika, “Ko e hā ʻaʻau, ʻoku ke haʻu
ton	Ko ia naʻa ne ʻomi ia ki hono fale, ʻo ne ʻatu ʻae meʻakai
ton	ki he fanga ʻasi; pea naʻa nau fufulu honau vaʻe, pea kai mo
ton	Pea ʻalu kituʻa ʻae kau tangata ʻo ʻIsileli ke tauʻi ʻa
ton	Penisimani; pea naʻe fakanofo ʻae tau ʻae fānau ʻa
ton	ʻIsileli ke tauʻi ʻakinautolu ʻi Kipea.
ton	Pea naʻe fuakava ʻae kau tangata ʻIsileli ʻi Misipa, ʻo
ton	pehē, “ʻOua naʻa ai ha tokotaha ʻiate kitautolu ʻe ʻatu
ton	hono ʻofefine kia Penisimani kenau mali.”
ton	Pea naʻe pekia ai ʻa Māloni mo Kilioni fakatouʻosi pē; pea
ton	naʻe toʻo pehē mei he fefine ʻa ʻene ongo tama mo hono
ton	Ke totongi ʻe Sihova ʻa hoʻo ngāue, pea ke foaki kiate koe
ton	ʻe Sihova ko e ʻOtua ʻo ʻIsileli ʻae totongi lahi, ʻaia ko
ton	e kapakau ʻoʻona kuo ke haʻu ke falala ki ai.”
ton	Pea pehē ʻe ia, “Ko ʻeku tama, ke ke nofo fiemālie pē, ke
ton	ʻoua ke ke ʻilo pe ngata fēfē ʻae meʻa ni: koeʻuhi ʻe
ton	ʻikai nofo noa pē ʻae tangata, kaeʻoua ke ne fakaʻosi ʻae
ton	Pea naʻe fakamamahi lahi ia ʻe hono fili, ke ne lāunga, ko e
ton	meʻa ʻi he tāpuni hono manāva ʻe Sihova.
ton	he ʻoku ʻikai ha tokotaha mo koe: pea ʻoku ʻikai foki ha
ton	makatuʻu ʻo hangē ko hotau ʻOtua.
ton	¶ Ka ko eni ko e fānau ʻoe angakovi ʻae ongo foha ʻo Ilai;
ton	naʻe ʻikai te na ʻilo ʻa Sihova.
ton	Pea naʻe lele ia kia Ilai, ʻo ne pehē, “Ko au eni; he naʻa
ton	ke ui au.” Pea pehē ʻe ia, “Naʻe ʻikai te u ui; ke ke
ton	toe tokoto.” Pea naʻe ʻalu ia ʻo tokoto.
ton	Pea ʻi heʻene hoko ki ai vakai naʻe nofo leʻo pe ʻa Ilai
ton	ʻi he nofoʻa ʻi he veʻehala: he naʻe tetetete hono loto
ton	telia ʻae puha tapu ʻoe ʻOtua. Pea ʻi he hoko ʻae tangata
ton	ki he kolo, ʻo fakahā ia, naʻe tangi kalanga ʻae kolo kotoa
ton	Pea ko ia, mou ngaohi ʻae saliote foʻou, pea toʻo ʻae ongo
ton	pulu fefine ʻoku huhuʻa, ʻaia kuo teʻeki hoko ki ai ha
ton	haʻamonga, pea nonoʻo ʻae ongo manu ki he saliote, pea ʻomi
ton	hona ʻuhiki ki ʻapi meiate kinaua:
ton	Pea naʻe fai ʻae fakamaau ʻe Samuela ki ʻIsileli ʻi he
ton	ngaahi ʻaho kotoa pē ʻo ʻene moʻui.
ton	Pea naʻe ʻalu ia, ʻo ʻasi ʻi he moʻunga ʻo ʻIfalemi, ʻo
ton	ne ʻosiki ʻae fonua ʻo Salisa, ka naʻe ʻikai te na ʻilo
ton	ʻakinautolu: pea naʻa na toki ō ʻo ʻasi ʻi he fonua ʻo
ton	Salima, pea naʻe ʻikai tenau ʻi ai: pea ʻalu ia ʻo ʻasi
ton	ʻi he fonua ʻoe kakai Penisimani, ka naʻe ʻikai te na ʻilo
ton	Pea ʻe hoko ʻae Laumālie ʻo Sihova kiate koe, pea te ke
ton	kikite koe mo kinautolu, pea ke liliu koe ko e tangata foʻou.
ton	Pea ʻi heʻene lau ʻakinautolu ʻi Piseki, naʻe toko tolu
ton	kilu ʻae fānau ʻa ʻIsileli pea toko tolu mano ʻae fānau
ton	He koeʻuhi ʻe ʻikai liʻaki ʻe Sihova ʻa hono kakai
ton	koeʻuhi ko hono huafa lahi: he kuo lelei kia Sihova ke ne
ton	ngaohi ʻakimoutolu ko hono kakai.
ton	Pea naʻe tatali ʻa Saula ʻi he potu ngataʻanga ʻo Kipea ʻi
ton	he lolo ʻakau ko e pomikanite ʻaia ʻoku ʻi Mikiloni: pea ko
ton	e kakai naʻe ʻiate ia ko e kau tangata ʻe toko onongeau nai;
ton	Pea naʻe ʻoho atu ʻae kakai ki he vete, ʻo toʻo ʻae fanga
ton	sipi, mo e fanga pulu, mo e kosi, ʻo tāmateʻi ia ʻi he
ton	kelekele: pea naʻe kai ia ʻe he kakai mo e toto.
ton	Ka naʻe fakamoʻui ʻe Saula mo e kakai ʻa Ekaki, mo e fanga
ton	sipi ʻoku fungani lelei, mo e fanga pulu, pea mo e fanga manu
ton	sino, pea mo e fanga lami, mo ia kotoa pē naʻe lelei, pea
ton	ʻikai siʻi fakaʻauha ʻakinautolu: ka ko ia kotoa pē naʻe
ton	mata kovi, mo taʻeʻaonga, ko ia ne nau fakaʻauha ʻaupito.
ton	Pea ke ui ʻa Sese ki he feilaulau, pea te u fakahā kiate koe
ton	ʻaia te ke fai: pea ke pani maʻaku ʻaia te u lau kiate koe.”
ton	Kapau ʻoku mafai ʻe ia ke ma tau mo au, pea ne tāmateʻi au,
ton	pehē te mau hoko ho hoʻomou kau tamaioʻeiki: pea kapau te u
ton	mālohi au kiate ia, ʻo tāmateʻi ia, te mou hoko ko ʻemau
ton	kau tamaioʻeiki, pea te mou tauhi ʻakimautolu.”
ton	Pea naʻe nonoʻo ʻe Tevita ʻene heletā ʻituʻa ki he kofu
ton	tau, ʻo ne ʻahiʻahi ke ʻalu; he naʻe teʻeki ai te ne
ton	ʻahiʻahiʻi ia. Pea naʻe pehē ʻe Tevita kia Saula, “ʻOku
ton	ʻikai te u faʻa ʻalu mo e nāunau ni: he kuo ʻikai te u
ton	ʻahiʻahiʻi ia.” Pea naʻe vete ia ʻe Tevita ʻo ne tuku ia.
ton	¶ Pea pongipongi hake, pea pehē, naʻe hoko kia Saula ʻae
ton	laumālie kovi mei he ʻOtua, pea naʻe kikite ia ʻi he loto
ton	fale: pea naʻe tā ʻe Tevita ʻaki hono nima ʻo hangē ko
ton	ʻene muʻaki fai: pea naʻe ʻi he nima ʻo Saula ʻae tao.
ton	Pea naʻe ʻia Saula ʻae laumālie kovi meia Sihova, ʻi
ton	heʻene nofo ʻi hono fale mo e tao ʻi hono nima: pea naʻe tā
ton	ʻe Tevita ʻaki hono nima.
ton	Pea te ke fakahā ʻe koe ʻae angaʻofa ʻa Sihova kiate au,
ton	ʻikai ʻi heʻeku kei moʻui ni pē, koeʻuhi ke ʻoua naʻaku
ton	Naʻe toki hoko ai ʻa Tevita ki Nopi ʻo ne ʻalu kia
ton	ʻAhimeleki ko e taulaʻeiki: pea manavahē ʻa ʻAhimeleki ʻi
ton	he fetaulaki mo Tevita, ʻo ne pehē kiate ia, “Ko e hā ʻoku
ton	ke tokotaha ai, pea ʻikai ha tangata ʻiate koe?”
ton	He ko ʻeku kamata fehuʻi ia ki he ʻOtua koeʻuhi ko ia? Ke
ton	mamaʻo ia ʻiate au: ke ʻoua naʻa tuku kovi ʻe he tuʻi ha
ton	meʻa ʻe taha ki heʻene tamaioʻeiki, pe ki he fale kotoa pē
ton	ʻo ʻeku tamai: he naʻe ʻikai ʻilo ʻe hoʻo tamaioʻeiki ha
ton	meʻa siʻi ʻi he meʻa ni kotoa pē, siʻi pe lahi.”
ton	Pea naʻe pehē ʻe Saula, “Ke monūʻia ʻakimoutolu ʻia
ton	Sihova; he ʻoku mou angaʻofa mai kiate au.
ton	Ko ia ke ke fuakava ni kiate au ʻia Sihova, ke ʻoua naʻa ke
ton	motuhi hoku hako kimui ʻiate au, pea ʻoua naʻa ke fakaʻauha
ton	hoku hingoa mei he fale ʻo ʻeku tamai.”
ton	‌ʻOku ou kole kiate koe, ke ke fakamolemole ʻae hala ʻa
ton	hoʻo kaunanga: he ko e moʻoni ʻe ngaohi ʻe Sihova ki hoku
ton	ʻeiki ʻae fale tuʻumaʻu; koeʻuhi ʻoku fai ʻe hoku ʻeiki
ton	ʻae ngaahi tau ʻa Sihova, pea naʻe ʻikai ʻilo ha kovi
ton	ʻiate koe ʻi ho ngaahi ʻaho kotoa pē.
ton	¶ Pea naʻe ʻalu ai ʻa Tevita ʻo laka ki he potu ʻe taha,
ton	pea tuʻu ia ki he tumutumu ʻoe moʻunga ʻo mamaʻo ai; ko e
ton	ʻataʻatā lahi naʻe ʻi hona vahaʻa:
ton	Pea fakakātoa fakataha ʻakinautolu ʻe he kakai Filisitia,
ton	ʻonau haʻu ʻo ʻapitanga ʻi Sunemi: pea naʻe fakakātoa
ton	fakataha ʻe Saula ʻa ʻIsileli kotoa pē, ʻonau haʻu ʻo
ton	¶ Pea naʻe pehē ʻe Tevita kia ʻAkisi, “Ka ko e hā ia kuo
ton	u fai? Pea ko e hā ia kuo ke ʻilo ki hoʻo tamaioʻeiki
ton	lolotonga ʻe tau nonofo mo koe ʻo aʻu ki he ʻaho ni,
ton	koeʻuhi ke ʻoua naʻaku ʻalu ʻo tauʻi ʻae ngaahi fili ʻo
ton	¶ Pea ʻi he hoko ʻa Tevita ki Sikilaki, naʻe fekau ʻe ia ke
ton	ʻatu ʻae koloa vete ki he kau mātuʻa ʻo Siuta, ʻio, ki
ton	hono ngaahi kāinga, ʻo pehē, “Vakai, ko e meʻaʻofa
ton	maʻamoutolu ʻi he vete mei he ngaahi fili ʻo Sihova;”
ton	Ko ia ne u tuʻu ki ai, ʻo tāmateʻi ia, koeʻuhi naʻaku
ton	ʻilo pau ʻe ʻikai te ne toe moʻui mei heʻene tō ki lalo
ton	ʻaupito: pea naʻaku toʻo ʻae tatā fakatuʻi mei hono ʻulu,
ton	mo e vesa mei hono nima, pea kuo u ʻomi ia ki heni ki hoku
ton	ʻaia naʻa ne ʻai ki hoʻomou kofu ʻae teunga ʻoe koula.
ton	Pea naʻe pehē ʻe ʻApina kiate ia, “Ke ke foki atu ki he
ton	toʻomataʻu pe ki hoʻo toʻohema, pea ke puke ha taha ʻoe kau
ton	talavou, pea ke maʻu ʻa hono mahafu.” Ka naʻe ʻikai afe
ton	atu ʻa ʻAsaeli mei tuli kiate ia.
ton	Pea ko eni fai ia: he kuo folofola ʻa Sihova ʻia Tevita, ʻo
ton	pehē, ‘ʻI he nima ʻo hoku tamaioʻeiki ko Tevita te u
ton	fakamoʻui ʻa hoku kakai ʻIsileli mei he nima ʻoe kau
ton	Filisitia, pea mei he nima ʻo honau ngaahi fili kotoa pē.’”
ton	Pea naʻa na ʻomi ʻae ʻulu ʻo Isiposeti kia Tevita ʻi
ton	Hepeloni, ʻo na pehē ki he tuʻi, “Vakai, ko e ʻulu eni ʻo
ton	Isiposeti ko e foha ʻo Saula, ko ho fili, ʻaia naʻe kumi ki
ton	hoʻo moʻui; pea kuo fai ʻe Sihova ʻae totongi ki heʻeku
ton	ʻeiki ko e tuʻi he ʻaho ni, ʻia Saula, pea mo hono hako.”
ton	Pea naʻe fai ia ʻe Tevita ʻo hangē ko ia naʻe fekau ʻe
ton	Sihova kiate ia; pea naʻe taaʻi ʻae kakai Filisitia mei Kepa
ton	ʻo aʻu atu ʻaupito ki Kesa.
ton	“ʻAlu ʻo tala ki heʻeku tamaioʻeiki ko Tevita, ‘ʻOku
ton	pehē ʻe Sihova, He te ke langa ʻe koe kiate au ha fale ke u
ton	Pea ʻi heʻene haʻu ʻae kakai Silia mei Tamasikusi ke tokoni
ton	kia Hetatesa ko e tuʻi ʻo Sopa, naʻe tāmateʻi ʻe Tevita
ton	ʻi he kakai Silia ʻae toko ua mano mo e toko ua afe.
ton	Pea naʻe pehē ai ʻe Tevita, “Te u fakahā ʻae ʻofa kia
ton	Hanuni ko e foha ʻo Naʻasi, koeʻuhi ko e fakahā ʻae ʻofa
ton	kiate au ʻe heʻene tamai.” Pea naʻe fekau atu ʻe Tevita
ton	ʻa ʻene kau tamaioʻeiki ke nau fakafiemālieʻi ia koeʻuhi
ton	ko ʻene tamai. Pea naʻe haʻu ʻae kau tamaioʻeiki ʻa Tevita
ton	ki he fonua ʻoe fānau ʻa ʻAmoni.
ton	Pea naʻe pehē ʻe Tevita kia ʻUlia, “Nofo ʻi heni he ʻaho
ton	ni foki, pea te u tuku koe ke ke ʻalu ʻapongipongi.” Ko ia
ton	naʻe nofo ai ʻa ʻUlia ʻi Selūsalema ʻi he ʻaho ko ia, mo
ton	Ka ko eni, koeʻuhi kuo ke tuku ha tuʻunga ʻi he meʻa ni ke
ton	lauʻikovi ai ʻa Sihova ʻe hono ngaahi fili, ʻe mate moʻoni
ton	ʻae tamasiʻi kuo fanauʻi kiate koe.”
ton	Pea naʻa ne pehēange ʻe ia, “ʻE ʻikai, ʻa hoku
ton	tuongaʻane, ʻoua naʻa ke fakamaaʻi au; he ʻoku ʻikai
ton	totonu ke fai ha meʻa pehē ʻi ʻIsileli: ʻoua naʻa ke fai
ton	Pea naʻe ʻalu ʻae fekau ʻa Soape ki Tikoa, ʻo ne ʻomi mei
ton	ai ʻae fefine poto, pea ne ne pehē kiate ia, “ʻOku ou kole
ton	kiate koe, ke ke fai ʻe koe ʻo hangē ko ha fefine tangi, pea
ton	ke ʻai eni ʻae kofu fakatauangaʻa, pea ʻoua naʻa ke tākai
ton	ʻaki koe ha lolo, ka ke hangē ko ha fefine kuo mamahi fuoloa
ton	Pea naʻe pehē ʻe ʻApisalomi kia Soape, “Vakai, naʻaku
ton	fekau atu kiate koe, ʻo pehē, Haʻu kiate au, koeʻuhi ke u
ton	fekau atu koe ki he tuʻi, ke pehē, ‘Ko e hā kuo u haʻu ai
ton	mei Kesuli? ʻE lelei pe ʻo ka ne u kei ʻi ai ni:’ kae tuku
ton	eni ke u mamata ki he fofonga ʻoe tuʻi; pea kapau ʻoku ʻiate
ton	au ha meʻa hala, tuku ke ne tāmateʻi au.”
ton	Vakai, te u nofo tatali pe au ʻi he potu tafangafanga ʻoe
ton	toafa, kaeʻoua ke ʻomi ha lea meiate kimoutolu ke fakamatala
ton	¶ Hili ia naʻe pehē ʻe ʻApisalomi kia ʻAhitofeli, “Mou
ton	fakakaukau ʻiate kimoutolu pe ko e hā te tau fai.”
ton	Ko ia naʻe nofo ai ʻa ʻIsileli mo ʻApisalomi ʻi he fonua
ton	Pea naʻe mamata ʻe he tangata leʻo ki he tangata kehe ʻe
ton	tokotaha ʻoku lele: pea naʻe ui ʻe he tangata leʻo ki he
ton	tangata naʻe tauhi matapā, ʻo ne pehē, “Vakai ʻoku lele
ton	mai tokotaha pe ʻae tangata kehe.” Pea naʻe pehē ʻe he
ton	tuʻi, “ʻOku ʻomi ʻae ongoongo ʻe ia foki.”
ton	Pea naʻe pehē ʻe Tevita, “Ko e hā kimoutolu kiate au,
ton	ʻakimoutolu ʻae ngaahi tama ʻo Seluia, ke mou hoko ai ko e
ton	ngaahi fili kiate au he ʻaho ni? He ʻe tāmateʻi ha tokotaha
ton	ʻi ʻIsileli ʻi he ʻaho ni? He ʻoku ʻikai te u ʻilo koā
ton	kuo u tuʻi au he ʻaho ni ki ʻIsileli?”
ton	Pea ʻi heʻenau hoko atu ki he fuʻu maka ʻaia ʻoku ʻi
ton	Kipione, naʻe muʻomuʻa atu ʻa ʻAmasa. Pea naʻe noʻotaki
ton	kiate ia ʻe Soape ʻa hono kofu naʻa ne ʻai, pea naʻe ʻai
ton	ki ai ʻae nonoʻo mo e heletā naʻe fakamaʻu ki ai mo hono
ton	ʻaiʻanga, ki hono tenga; pea ʻi heʻene ʻalu atu naʻe tō
ton	Pea naʻe tala kia Tevita ʻae meʻa naʻe fai ʻe Lisipa koe
ton	taʻahine ʻo ʻAia koe sinifu ʻo Saula.
ton	Naʻa ne fakamoʻui au mei hoku fili mālohi, pea meiate
ton	kinautolu naʻe fehiʻa kiate au: he naʻa nau mālohi fau kiate
ton	Ko e ʻOtua ia ʻaia ʻoku fai ʻae totongi maʻaku, mo ne
ton	fakamoʻulaloa ʻae kakai kiate au,
ton	Ko Ilesi ko e tangata Paleti, mo Ila ko e foha ʻo Ikesi ko e
ton	Pea ʻi heʻene mafao atu ʻe he ʻāngelo ʻa hono nima ki
ton	Selūsalema ke fakaʻauha ia, naʻe liliu ʻa Sihova mei he
ton	fakahoko ʻae kovi, pea ne folofola ki he ʻāngelo ʻaia naʻe
ton	tāmateʻi ʻae kakai, “Kuo lahi; ke taʻofi eni ho nima.”
ton	Pea naʻe feʻunga ʻae ʻāngelo ʻo Sihova mo e hahaʻanga
ton	uite ʻo ʻAlauna ko e tangata Sepusi.
ton	Pea ko koe, ʻe hoku ʻeiki ko e tuʻi, kuo hanga mai kiate koe
ton	ʻae mata kotoa pē ʻo ʻIsileli, koeʻuhi ke ke fakahā kiate
ton	kinautolu pe ko hai ia ʻe hoko mo koe ke nofo ki he nofoʻa
ton	fakatuʻi ʻo hoku ʻeiki ko e tuʻi.
ton	Pea naʻe manavahē ʻa ʻAtunaisa koeʻuhi ko Solomone, pea
ton	naʻa ne tuʻu hake, mo ne ʻalu ʻo ne puke ki he nifo ʻoe
ton	Pea naʻe pehē ʻe he tuʻi kia ʻApaiata ko e taulaʻeiki,
ton	“ʻAlu ko e ki ʻAnatoti, ki ho potu fonua ʻoʻou; he ʻoku
ton	totonu ke ke mate koe; ka ʻe ʻikai te u tāmateʻi koe ʻi he
ton	kuonga ni, koeʻuhi naʻa ke fua ʻae puha tapu ʻa Sihova ko e
ton	ʻOtua ʻi he ʻao ʻo Tevita ko ʻeku tamai, pea koeʻuhi naʻa
ton	ke mamahi koe ʻi he meʻa kotoa pē naʻe mamahi ai ʻa ʻeku
ton	Ko ia ke ke tuku ki hoʻo tamaioʻeiki ha loto poto ke
ton	fakamaauʻi ʻa hoʻo kakai, koeʻuhi ke u faʻa ʻilo totonu
ton	ʻae lelei mo e kovi; he ko hai ʻoku faʻa fai ke fakamaauʻi
ton	eni ʻa hoʻo kakai tokolahi ni?”
ton	Ko e foha ʻo Hesiti, ʻi ʻAlupoti; naʻe ʻaʻana ʻa Soko,
ton	pea mo e fonua kotoa pē ʻo Hefeli:
ton	Pea vakai, ʻoku ou pehē ke langa ha fale ki he huafa ʻo
ton	Sihova ko hoku ʻOtua, ʻo hangē ko e folofola ʻa Sihova kia
ton	Tevita ko ʻeku tamai, ʻo pehē, ‘Ko ho ʻalo, ʻaia te u
ton	fakanofo ki ho nofoʻa fakatuʻi ke fetongi koe, ʻe langa ʻe
ton	ia ha fale ki hoku huafa.’
ton	Pea naʻa ne ʻaofi ʻae holisi ʻoe fale, ko e hanga ʻe
ton	fāngofulu ʻaki ʻae laupapa sita, ʻio, ʻae faliki pea mo e
ton	holisi; naʻa ne ngaohi pehē ia ki loto maʻae folofolaʻanga,
ton	pea mo e potu toputapu ʻaupito.
ton	¶ Pea naʻa ne ngaohi foki ʻae fakamalumaluʻanga ki he
ton	nofoʻa fakaʻeiʻeiki ke ne fai mei ai ʻae fakamaau, ʻio,
ton	ʻae fale fakamalumalu ʻoe fakamaauʻanga: pea naʻe ʻufiʻufi
ton	ia ʻaki ʻae sita mei he potu faliki fale ʻe taha ki he taha
ton	Naʻe pehē ni ʻa ʻene ngaohi ʻae tuʻunga ʻe hongofulu:
ton	naʻe tatau pe ʻa honau haka, mo honau fakafuofua, pea mo honau
ton	Pea naʻa ne pehē, “Fakafetaʻi kia Sihova ko e ʻOtua ʻo
ton	ʻIsileli ʻaia naʻe folofola mei hono fofonga ki heʻeku tamai
ton	ko Tevita, pea kuo ne fakamoʻoni ia ʻaki ʻa hono nima, ʻi
ton	Ke ke toki fanongo ʻe koe ʻi he langi ki heʻenau lotu mo
ton	ʻenau kole, pea ke tokonia ʻakinautolu ʻi he meʻa totonu.
ton	Pea ko e meʻa ʻi he fale ni, ʻoku māʻolunga ni, ko ia kotoa
ton	pē ʻoku ʻalu ofi ki ai, ʻe ofo ai mo fakaʻiseʻisa; pea te
ton	nau pehē, ‘Ko e hā kuo fai pehē ai ʻe Sihova ki he fonua
ton	Fakafetaʻi kia Sihova ko ho ʻOtua, ʻaia kuo lōlōfie lelei
ton	ʻiate koe, ke fakanofo koe ki he nofoʻa fakatuʻi ʻi
ton	ʻIsileli: koeʻuhi naʻe ʻofa taʻengata ʻa Sihova ki
ton	ʻIsileli, ko ia kuo ne fakanofo ai koe ko e tuʻi, ke fai ʻae
ton	fakamaau mo e fai totonu.”
ton	¶ Pea naʻe houhau ʻa Sihova kia Solomone, koeʻuhi naʻe
ton	fakatafoki ʻa hono loto meia Sihova ko e ʻOtua ʻo ʻIsileli,
ton	ʻaia naʻe ha tuʻo ua mai kiate ia,
ton	Pea koeʻuhi ko e meʻa ni te u fakamamahiʻi ʻae hako ʻo
ton	Tevita, ka ʻe ʻikai ke taʻengata.’”
ton	¶ Hili ia naʻe langa hake ʻe Selopoami ʻa Sikemi ʻi he
ton	moʻunga ko ʻIfalemi, pea ne nofo ʻi ai; pea naʻa ne ʻalu
ton	atu mei ai ʻo ne langa hake ʻa Penieli.
ton	Pea naʻa ne ui ki he tangata ʻoe ʻOtua ʻaia naʻe haʻu mei
ton	Siuta, ʻo pehē, “ʻOku pehē ʻe Sihova, Koeʻuhi kuo ke
ton	talangataʻa ki he folofola ʻa Sihova, pea kuo ʻikai te ke fai
ton	ʻae fekau ʻaia naʻe fekau kiate koe ʻe Sihova ko ho ʻOtua,
ton	Pea te ne liʻaki ʻa ʻIsileli koeʻuhi ko e ngaahi angahala
ton	ʻa Selopoami, ʻaia naʻe fai angahala ʻe ia, pea naʻa ne
ton	fakaangahalaʻi ʻa ʻIsileli.”
ton	Ka naʻe ʻikai liʻaki ʻae ngaahi potu māʻolunga: ka neongo
ton	ia naʻe angatonu kia Sihova ʻae loto ʻo ʻAsa ʻi hono ngaahi
ton	Pea naʻe lapasi ia ʻe heʻene tamaioʻeiki ko Simili, ko e
ton	ʻeiki naʻe pule ki hono vahe ua mālie ʻo ʻene ngaahi
ton	saliote, lolotonga ʻa ʻene ʻi Tilisa, mo ʻene inu ke kona
ton	ʻi he fale ʻo ʻAlisa ko e tauhi ʻo hono fale ʻi Tilisa.
ton	Pea ʻe hoko ʻo pehē, te ke inu ai mei he vaitafe; pea kuo u
ton	fekau ki he fanga leveni ke fafangaʻi koe ʻi ai.”
ton	Pea naʻa ne pehē, “Ko e hā ʻa ʻeku fai hala, ke ke
ton	tukuange ai ʻa hoʻo tamaioʻeiki ki he nima ʻo ʻEhapi ke
ton	Pea ʻi he mamata ʻae kakai ki ai, naʻa nau tō hifo ki honau
ton	mata: pea naʻa nau pehē, “Ko Sihova, ko e ʻOtua pe ia; ko
ton	Sihova ko e ʻOtua pe ia.”
ton	1 ʻOku kāpui ʻa Samēlia ʻaki ʻae kautau ʻo Peni-Hatati.
ton	13 Ko e tāmateʻi ʻae kakai Silia. 22 ʻOku toe tauʻi ʻa
ton	ʻEhapi ʻe he kakai Silia ʻi. 28 ʻOku toe tauʻi ʻae kakai
ton	Silia pea ʻoku fakavaivai kinautolu ʻe ʻEhapi. 31 Ko e
ton	fuakava ʻa ʻEhapi mo Peni-Hatati. 35 ʻOku fakahā ʻae
ton	fakamalaʻia mei he ʻOtua kia ʻEhapi.
ton	Ka naʻe feholaki ʻae toenga ki ʻEfeki, ki he loto kolo; pea
ton	naʻe hinga ʻae ā ʻi ai ʻo taʻomia ʻae kau tangata ʻe
ton	toko ua mano mo e toko fitu afe, ʻaia naʻe toe. Pea naʻe hola

ton	tuʻu hake ʻa ʻEhapi ke ne ʻalu hifo ki he ngoue vaine ʻo

ton	ko ia pe ʻoku moʻoni ʻi he huafa ʻo Sihova?”
ton	Pea ko e toenga kakai angafakasotoma ʻaia naʻe toe ʻi he
ton	ngaahi ʻaho ʻo ʻene tamai ko ʻAsa, naʻa ne ʻave mei he

ton	“ʻOku ke ʻilo ʻe ʻave ʻe Sihova ʻa hoʻo ʻeiki mei ho
ton	ʻulu he ʻaho ni?” Pea naʻe pehē ʻe ia, “ʻIo, ʻoku ou
ton	ʻilo; ka mou longo pe kimoutolu.”
ton	Pea naʻa ne ʻalu mo ne fekau kia Sihosafate, ko e tuʻi ʻo
ton	Siuta, ʻo pehē, “Kuo angatuʻu kiate au ʻae tuʻi ʻo
ton	Moape: te ke fie ʻalu mo au ki Moape ke fai ʻae tau pe ʻikai?
ton	Pea naʻe pehē mai ʻe ia, Te u ʻalu hake pe; ʻoka kou hangē
ton	ko koe, ʻoku tatau ʻa hoku kakai mo ho kakai, pea tatau ʻa
ton	ʻeku fanga hoosi mo hoʻo fanga hoosi.”
ton	Pea naʻe pehē ʻe he fefine ki hono husepāniti, “Vakai mai,
ton	ʻoku ou ʻilo ko e tangata māʻoniʻoni eni ʻoe ʻOtua, ʻaia
ton	ʻoku afe mai kiate kitaua maʻuaipē.
ton	Pea naʻe ʻalu ha tokotaha ki he ngoue ke tānaki ʻae
ton	louʻakau, pea naʻa ne ʻilo ai ʻae vaine tupu vao, pea naʻa
ton	ne tānaki mei ai ʻae ngaahi fua ke pito ai hono kofu, pea
ton	naʻa ne ʻomi ʻo hifi ia ki he kulo ʻoe haka lū: he naʻe
ton	ʻikai te nau ʻilo hono anga.
ton	Pea ʻi heʻene hoko atu ki he fale leʻo, naʻa ne toʻo ia mei

ton	ongo tangata ke ʻalu, pea naʻa na ʻalu.
ton	Pea lolotonga ʻae ʻalu ange ʻae tuʻi ʻo ʻIsileli ʻi he
ton	funga ʻā, naʻe tangi mai kiate ia ha fefine, ʻo pehē,
ton	“ʻE hoku ʻeiki, ko e tuʻi, tokoni mai.”
ton	Pea naʻe toki lea ʻa ʻIlaisa ki he fefine, ʻaia naʻa ne

ton	hake, pea ʻalu ʻa koe mo ho kau nofoʻanga, pea ʻāunofo ʻi
ton	ha potu pe te ke faʻa ʻāunofo ki ai: he kuo pau pe meia
ton	Sihova ke ʻai ha honge; pea ʻe hoko foki ia ki he fonua ʻi he
ton	Pea naʻe ui mai ʻe ʻIlaisa ha tokotaha ʻi he fānau ʻae kau
ton	palōfita, mo ne pehē kiate ia, “Nonoʻo ho noʻotanga vala,
ton	mo ke ʻave ʻi ho nima ʻae puha ni ʻoe lolo, pea ke ʻalu ki

ton	naʻa ne pehē, “Naʻe lelei koā ʻa Simili, ʻaia naʻa ne

ton	Pea naʻe ʻalu ʻa Sehu, mo Sonatapi ko e foha ʻo Lekapi, ki

ton	kimoutolu ha taha ʻi he kau tamaioʻeiki ʻa Sihova, ka ko e
ton	Pea naʻa nau puke nima ia; pea naʻa ne ʻalu ʻi he hala ko ia
ton	naʻe faʻa hū ai ʻae fanga hoosi ki he nofoʻanga ʻoe tuʻi:
ton	pea naʻe tāmateʻi ia ʻi ai.
ton	Pea naʻa ne fai ʻae meʻa naʻe kovi ʻi he ʻao ʻo Sihova,
ton	pea naʻa ne muimui ki he ngaahi angahala ʻa Selopoami ko e
ton	foha ʻo Nipati, ʻaia naʻe fakaangahalaʻi ʻa ʻIsileli naʻe
ton	ʻikai te ne mahuʻi mei ai.
ton	Ka naʻe ʻikai tāmateʻi ʻe ia ʻae fānau ʻae kau fakapō:

ton	ʻaia naʻe fekau ai ʻe Sihova, ʻo pehē, “ʻE ʻikai
ton	tāmateʻi ʻae tamai koeʻuhi ko e fānau, pe tāmateʻi ʻae
ton	fānau koeʻuhi ko ʻenau ngaahi tamai; ka ʻe tāmateʻi ʻae
ton	tangata taki taha koeʻuhi ko ʻene angahala ʻaʻana pe.”
ton	Pea ko hono toe ʻoe ngaahi ngāue ʻa ʻAsalia mo ia kotoa pē
ton	naʻa ne fai, ʻikai ʻoku tohi ia ʻi he tohi fakamatala ki he
ton	¶ Pea ko hono toe ʻoe ngaahi ngāue ʻa Sotami, mo ia kotoa
ton	pē naʻa ne fai, ʻikai kuo tohi ia ʻi he tohi fakamatala ki
ton	Pea ʻi hono hiva ʻoe taʻu ʻo Hosea naʻe lavaʻi ʻa

ton	ia te mou manavahē ki ai, pea ko ia ia te mou lotu ki ai, pea
ton	ko ia ia te mou fai ki ai ʻae feilaulau.
ton	Pea ʻe fēfeeʻi hao faʻa fai ke fakafoki ʻae mata ʻoe
ton	ʻeikitau ʻe tokotaha, ko e siʻi hifo taha pe ʻi he kau

ton	he ngaahi saliote mo e kau tangata heka hoosi?
ton	‌ʻE Sihova, punou hifo ho fofonga, pea ke fakafanongo: ʻe
ton	Sihova fakaʻā ho fofonga, pea ke ʻafioʻi: pea ongoʻi ʻae
ton	ngaahi lea ʻa Senakalipe, ʻaia kuo ne fekau mai ia ke lea kovi
ton	¶ Pea naʻe pehē ʻe Hesekaia kia ʻIsaia, “Ko e hā hono
ton	fakaʻilonga ʻoe fakamoʻui au, pea ki heʻeku ʻalu hake ki he
ton	fale ʻo Sihova ʻi hono tolu ʻoe ʻaho?”
ton	Ka ko eni, naʻe lingi ʻe Manase ʻae toto māʻoniʻoni ʻo
ton	lahi ʻaupito, mo ne fakafonu ʻaki ia ʻa Selūsalema mei he

ton	angahala ʻaia naʻa ne fakaangahala ai ʻa Siuta, ʻi he fai

ton	Koeʻuhi naʻe ongongofua ho loto, pea kuo ke fakavaivaiʻi koe
ton	ʻi he ʻao ʻo Sihova, ʻi hoʻo fanongo ʻaia naʻaku lea ki
ton	ai ki he potu ni, pea ki hono kakai, koeʻuhi ke nau hoko ko e
ton	ʻauhia, mo e malaʻia, pea kuo ke haehae ho ngaahi kofu, pea
ton	tangi ʻi hoku ʻao; ʻoku pehē ʻe Sihova, Kuo u ongoʻi koe

ton	mei hono ʻao, naʻe fai ʻae angatuʻu ʻa Setikia ki he tuʻi

ton	kai mā ia ʻi hono ʻao ʻi he ngaahi ʻaho kotoa pē ʻo ʻene
ton	Ko e ngaahi foha ʻo ʻEpalahame; ko ʻAisake, mo ʻIsimeʻeli.
ton	¶ Ko e ngaahi foha eni ʻo Siuta; ko ʻEa, mo ʻOnani, mo Sila:

ton	Pea ko e ngaahi foha ʻo Sonatane; ko Peleti, mo Sasa. Ko e

ton	pea mo ʻUsili, ko e ngaahi foha ʻo Isi.
ton	Ko kinautolu ni ko e ngaahi foha ʻo Livai; ko Kesoni, mo
ton	¶ Pea ko kinautolu eni naʻe tuku ʻe Tevita ke ʻanautolu ʻae
ton	fai ʻae hiva ʻi he fale ʻo Sihova, hili ʻae hoko ʻae puha

ton	vaikeli ʻi Petelihema, ʻaia ʻoku ʻi he veʻematapā!”
ton	Mo Ilieli, mo ʻOpeti, mo Sesieli ko e tangata Mesopaia.

ton	honau tokolahi, ʻae tauhi ʻi he fale ʻo Saula.
ton	¶ Pea naʻe toe fakatokolahi ʻe Tevita ʻa hono ngaahi uaifi
ton	ʻi Selūsalema: pea naʻe toe tupu ʻia Tevita ʻae ngaahi foha
ton	mo e ngaahi ʻofefine kehe.
ton	Pea naʻe fua ʻae puha ʻoe fuakava ʻae ʻOtua ʻe he fānau

ton	hangē ko e fekau ʻe Mōsese ʻo fakatatau mo e folofola ʻa
ton	tuku ke fiefia ʻae loto ʻokinautolu, ʻoku kumi kia Sihova.
ton	ʻoku taau mo ia foki ʻae manavahē ke lahi hake ʻi he ngaahi

ton	He ko koe, ʻE hoku ʻOtua, kuo ke fakahā ki hoʻo tamaioʻeiki
ton	te ke langa ha fale moʻona: ko ia kuo loto ai ʻa hoʻo
ton	tamaioʻeiki ke lotu ʻi ho ʻao.
ton	Pea naʻe hū mai kituʻa ʻae fānau ʻa ʻAmoni mo nau

ton	nofo kehe fakataha ʻae ngaahi tuʻi naʻe haʻu, ʻi he potu
ton	“Ke ke ʻalu ʻo tala kia Tevita, ʻo pehē, ʻOku pehē ʻe
ton	Sihova, ʻOku ou tuku atu ʻae meʻa ko eni ʻe tolu, pea ke
ton	fili ʻe koe ha taha ʻi ai, koeʻuhi ke u fai ia kiate koe.
ton	‘Vakai, ʻe fanauʻi kiate koe ha foha, ʻaia ʻe hoko ko e
ton	tangata ʻoe melino; pea te u tuku kiate ia ʻae mālōlō mei
ton	hono ngaahi fili kotoa pē ʻoku nofo takatakai hake; koeʻuhi
ton	ʻe fakahingoa ia ko Solomone, pea te u foaki ʻae melino mo e

ton	he kuo nau fakataʻeʻaongaʻi hoʻo fono.

ton	pea ʻe muʻomuʻa ʻi ho ʻao ʻa hoʻo māʻoniʻoni;
ton	pea te u ngaohi koe ke ke heka ʻi he ngaahi potu māʻolunga
ton	ʻoku ʻi honau ngaahi hala ʻae maumau mo e fakaʻauha.
ton	‌ʻIo, kuo mole ʻae moʻoni;
ton	pea ʻe hā hono nāunau ʻiate koe.
ton	“Pea ʻe toe langa ho ʻa ʻe he ngaahi foha ʻoe muli,
ton	‌ʻE ʻikai toe hoko ʻae laʻā ko hoʻo maama ʻi he ʻaho;
ton	pea mo e ngoue ʻoku ne fakatupu hake ʻae ngaahi meʻa ʻoku

ton	meʻakai ki ho ngaahi fili;
ton	pea moeʻi ʻakinautolu ʻi hoku houhau lahi;
ton	Pea naʻa ne manatu ki he ngaahi ʻaho ʻi muʻa,
ton	1 ʻOku hū ʻae siasi ke hā ʻae mālohi ʻoe ʻOtua. 5 ʻI he
ton	manatu ki he ʻaloʻofa ʻoe ʻOtua, ʻoku fakahā ia ʻae kovi
ton	ʻoe loto taʻeliliu. 9 ʻOku lāunga ia ʻi heʻenau mamahi.
ton	‌ʻOua naʻa ke houhau lahi, ʻE Sihova,
ton	ko e afi ʻoku ulo ʻi he ʻaho kotoa pē.
ton	mo fili ʻaia naʻe ʻikai te u fiemālie ai.
ton	he ko ia ʻe mate ʻi hono teau taʻu ʻe mate ko e tamasiʻi pe;
ton	ko ia ʻoku ne feilaulau ʻaki ha lami, ʻo hangē kuo ne
ton	tuʻusi ke motu ʻae kia ʻoe kulī;
ton	‌ʻOku pehē ʻe Sihova, “ʻO hangē ko e tuʻumaʻu ʻi
ton	hoku ʻao, ʻae ngaahi langi foʻou pea mo e maama foʻou, ʻaia
ton	te u ngaohi, ʻe pehē ʻae tuʻumaʻu ʻo homou hako mo homou
ton	Pea te nau tauʻi koe; ka ʻe ʻikai te nau mālohi kiate
ton	koe;” he ʻoku pehē mai ʻe Sihova, “ʻOku ou ʻiate koe,
ton	pea naʻe angatuʻu kiate au ʻae kau tauhi foki,
ton	ko ia ke ke ʻilo mo vakai, ko e meʻa kovi mo fakamamahi,
ton	Ko kinautolu ʻoku pehē ki he ʻakau, ‘Ko ʻeku tamai koe;’
ton	koeʻuhi ʻoku ke pehē, ‘Naʻe ʻikai te ke fai kovi.’
ton	“Vakai, ʻoku mau haʻu kiate koe; he ko koe ko Sihova ko
ton	Ne u mamata, pea vakai, kuo toafa ʻae potu fua lelei, pea kuo
ton	maumauʻi hifo ʻae ngaahi kolo kotoa pē ʻi he ʻao ʻo
ton	Sihova, ʻi hono houhau kakaha.
ton	Pea naʻe ʻikai te nau pehē ʻi honau loto, ‘Ko eni, ke tau
ton	manavahē kia Sihova ko hotau ʻOtua, ʻaia ʻoku ne foaki kiate
ton	kitautolu ʻae ʻuha muʻa mo e ʻuha mui, ʻi hono ʻaho
ton	totonu: pea kuo ne tauhi maʻatautolu ʻae ngaahi uike
ton	tuʻutuʻuni ki he ututaʻu.’
ton	He naʻa nau mā ʻi heʻenau fai meʻa fakalielia?
ton	Kuo hoko ʻae fale ni, ʻaia ʻoku ui ʻi hoku huafa, ko e
ton	ʻananga ʻoe kau kaihaʻa ʻi homou ʻao?” ʻOku pehē ʻe
ton	Sihova, “Vakai kuo u mamata ʻeau ki ai.”
ton	Te ne ʻalu atu pea ʻe ʻikai toe foki mai?
ton	ʻIkai ʻoku ai ha faitoʻo ʻi ai?
ton	“Vakai, Te u fakavela ke vai ʻakinautolu, pea ʻahiʻahiʻi
ton	He ʻoku ongo mai mei Saione ʻae leʻo ʻoe tangi,

ton	ko honau kofu ʻoku ʻuliʻuli mo kulokula:

ton	he kau tangata ʻo Siuta, pea mo e kakai ʻo Selūsalema;

ton	heletā; pea ʻe mate honau ngaahi foha, mo honau ngaahi
ton	kuo nau kalanga mo tuli kiate koe:

ton	ʻakinautolu ko e tangata taki taha ki hono ʻapi, pea ko e
ton	tangata taki taha ki hono fonua.
ton	pea ʻe tafe hifo ʻae ngaahi loʻimata,

ton	Te nau mate ʻi he ngaahi mate kovi; pea ʻe ʻikai ha tangi
ton	koeʻuhi ko kinautolu; pea ʻe ʻikai tanu ʻakinautolu; ka te
ton	nau hangē ko e kinohaʻa ʻi he funga ʻoe fonua: pea ʻe
ton	fakaʻauha ʻakinautolu ʻe he heletā, mo e honge: pea ʻe kai

ton	tuku ke u mamata ki ho houhau kiate kinautolu:

ton	ka ko e moʻoni te u ngaohi koe ko e toafa,

ton	pea ʻe ʻikai monūʻia ha tangata ʻi hono hako,
ton	KO SIHOVA KO HOTAU MĀʻONIʻONI.
ton	‌ʻE fēfē hono fuoloa ʻoe meʻa ni ʻi he loto ʻoe kau
ton	palōfita ʻoku kikite ʻaki ʻae ngaahi loi? ʻio, ko e kau

ton	fekau ʻakinautolu: ka kuo ʻikai te mou fanongo, pe fakatokanga
ton	te ne ngungulu lahi ʻi hono ʻafioʻanga;
ton	he kuo maumauʻi ʻe Sihova ʻenau ngoue.

ton	Sihova ko Ulisa ko e foha ʻo Semaia mei Kesa-Sialimi, ʻaia
ton	naʻe kikite ki he kolo ni, pea ki he fonua ni, ʻo hangē ko e

ton	ʻIsileli, “Kuo u maumauʻi ʻae haʻamonga ʻae tuʻi ʻo
ton	Pea ʻoku pehē ʻe Sihova, Te mou ʻilo au: pea te u liliu
ton	homou fakapōpula, pea te u tānaki ʻakimoutolu mei he ngaahi
ton	puleʻanga kotoa pē, pea mei he ngaahi potu kotoa pē naʻaku
ton	kapusi ʻakimoutolu ki ai, ʻoku pehē ʻe Sihova; pea te u toe
ton	ʻomi ʻakimoutolu mei he potu ko ia naʻaku pule ke fetuku
ton	pōpula ki ai ʻakimoutolu.’
ton	ʻaia naʻaku foaki ki heʻenau ngaahi tamai,
ton	Ko ia ʻe fakaʻauha ʻakinautolu kotoa pē ʻoku fakaʻauha koe;
ton	he ko hai eni naʻa ne ueʻi hono loto ke haʻu kiate au?
ton	ʻe toe teuteu ʻaki koe ho ngaahi meʻa faiva,

ton	e motuʻa fakataha: he te u liliu ʻenau mamahi ko e fiefia, pea
ton	te u fakafiemālieʻi ʻakinautolu pea fakafiefiaʻi
ton	ʻakinautolu ʻi he hili ʻenau mamahi.
ton	He naʻe kāpui ʻa Selūsalema ʻe he kau tau ʻae tuʻi ʻo
ton	Papilone ʻi he ngaahi ʻaho ko ia: pea naʻe tuku ʻa Selemaia
ton	ko e palōfita ki he lotoʻā ʻoe fale fakapōpula, ʻaia naʻe
ton	ʻi he fale ʻoe tuʻi ʻo Siuta.
ton	He kuo hoko kiate au ʻae kolo ni ko e tupuʻanga ʻo ʻeku
ton	tuputāmaki mo hoku houhau talu mei he ʻaho naʻa nau langa ai
ton	ia ʻo aʻu ki he ʻaho ni; koeʻuhi ke u hiki ia mei hoku ʻao,
ton	te u fakatupu kia Tevita ʻae vaʻa ʻoe māʻoniʻoni;
ton	‌ʻOka hili ʻae taʻu ʻe fitu te mou tukuange ʻae tangata
ton	taki taha hono tokoua ko e Hepelū, ʻaia kuo fakatau kiate koe,

ton	tukuange ia ke ne tauʻatāina meiate koe: ka naʻe ʻikai
ton	fanongo kiate au ʻa hoʻomou ngaahi tamai, pe fakafanongo mai
ton	Pea naʻe hoko ʻo pehē ʻi hono fā ʻoe taʻu ʻo Sihoiakimi

ton	ʻo pehē, “Ko e hā naʻa ke tohi ai? ʻo pehē, ‘Ko e
ton	moʻoni ʻe haʻu ʻae tuʻi ʻo Papilone ʻo fakaʻauha ʻae
ton	fonua ni pea fakatangaʻi ʻae tangata pea mo e manu?’””
ton	“ʻOku pehē mai ʻa Sihova, ‘Ko ia ʻoku nofo ʻi he kolo
ton	ni, te ne mate ʻi he heletā, mo e honge, pea mo e mahaki

ton	moʻui; ʻe ʻiate ia ʻene moʻui ko e koloa kuo vetea, pea te
ton	Pea naʻe haʻu ʻae houʻeiki kotoa pē kia Selemaia pea
ton	fehuʻi kiate ia: pea ne fakahā kiate kinautolu, ʻo hangē ko
ton	e ngaahi lea ni kotoa pē ʻaia naʻe fekau ʻe he tuʻi. Pea
ton	naʻe ʻikai te nau toe lea kiate ia; he naʻe ʻikai ke hā mai
ton	Naʻa nau haʻu kia Ketalia ʻi Misipa, ʻio, ko ʻIsimeʻeli ko
ton	e foha ʻo Natania, pea ko Sohanani mo Sonatani ko e ongo foha
ton	ʻo Kalia, pea ko Selaia ko e foha ʻo Tanumeti, pea ko e ngaahi
ton	foha ʻo ʻIfai ko e tangata Nitofa, pea mo Seasania ko e foha

ton	1 ʻOku tokanga ʻa Sohanani ke ʻeke ʻe Selemaia ki he ʻOtua,
ton	pea ne fakahā te ne fai talangofua kia Sihova. 7 ʻOku fakahā
ton	ʻe Selemaia ʻe maluʻi ia ʻi Siuta, 13 Kae fakaʻauha ʻi
ton	ʻIsipite. 19 ʻOku ne valoki ki heʻenau kākā, ʻi heʻenau
ton	kole kia Sihova ʻaia naʻe ʻikai te nau loto ki ai.
ton	Pea naʻa nau ʻalu ki he fonua ko ʻIsipite: he naʻe ʻikai te
ton	nau talangofua ki he leʻo ʻo Sihova: pea naʻa nau aʻu ki
ton	Koeʻuhi kuo mou tutu ʻae meʻa namu kakala, pea koeʻuhi kuo
ton	mou angahala kia Sihova, pea ʻikai talangofua ki he leʻo ʻo
ton	Sihova, pe ʻeveʻeva ʻi heʻene ngaahi fono, pe ʻi heʻene
ton	ngaahi tuʻutuʻuni, pe ʻi heʻene ngaahi fakamoʻoni; ko ia

ton	pea fakahā ʻi Nofe mo Tapanesi:

ton	Pea mo Tiponi, mo Nipo, pea mo Petetipilateimi,
ton	pea te ne mafao atu hono kapakau ki Moape.
ton	pea nofo ʻa hono kakai ʻi hono ngaahi kolo?
ton	koeʻuhi te u ʻomi kiate ia ʻae tuʻutāmaki ʻo ʻIsoa, ko e
ton	ʻaho te u ʻaʻahi ai kiate ia.
ton	te u fakahifo koe mei ai,” ʻoku pehē ʻe Sihova.
ton	kuo tafoki mai ia ke hola,
ton	kuo laiki ʻaupito hono ngaahi meʻa fakatātā.’
ton	pea ʻomi ki Papilone, ʻae fakataha ʻoe ngaahi puleʻanga lahi
ton	fai kiate ia, ʻo hangē ko ʻene fai ʻe ia.
ton	‌ʻE Papilone kuo u ʻai ʻae tauhele kiate koe,
ton	he kuo hokosia mai ho ʻaho,
ton	pea mo e fanga manu hehengi ʻoe ngaahi motu,
ton	ko e moʻoni ʻe ʻave ʻakinautolu ʻe he siʻi hifo:
ton	ko ia kuo faha ai ʻae ngaahi puleʻanga.
ton	pea te nau fai ʻae kalanga kiate koe.’
ton	ʻae talavou pea mo e taʻahine.
ton	kuo nau liliu ʻo hangē ko e kau fefine:
ton	pea ʻe ʻikai ʻi ai ha kakai.
ton	mo e fakamālohi ʻi he fonua,
ton	Koeʻuhi kuo hoko ʻae maumau kiate ia,
ton	Pea ʻi hono fā māhina, ʻi hono ʻaho ʻe hiva ʻoe māhina,
ton	naʻe lahi ʻaupito ʻae honge ʻi he kolo, koeʻuhi naʻe
ton	ʻikai ha meʻakai ki he kakai ʻoe fonua.
ton	Pea ko ʻene meʻakai, naʻe tufa maʻuaipē ʻe he tuʻi ʻo
ton	Papilone ʻae kai kiate ia, ko e ʻinasi ʻi he ʻaho kotoa pē,
ton	ʻi he ʻaho kotoa pē ʻo ʻene moʻui, ʻo aʻu ki he ʻaho
ton	pea kuo nau hola taʻehamālohi ʻi he ʻao ʻo ia ʻoku tuli.
ton	kuo ne ngaohi au ko e liʻaki mo e vaivai ʻi he ʻaho kotoa pē.
ton	kuo liliu hoku loto ʻiate au;
ton	pea ne tāmateʻi ʻakinautolu kotoa pē naʻe hoihoifua
ton	ko e kau tāupoʻou ʻo Selūsalema ʻoku nau fakatōmapeʻe
ton	honau ʻulu ʻo aʻu ki he kelekele.
ton	kuo ne fakamoʻoni ki heʻene folofola ʻaia naʻa ne fekau ʻi
ton	Ko e moʻoni kuo ne liliu kiate au,
ton	Pea ne u pehē, “Ko ʻeku mālohi
ton	Ke kākaaʻi ʻae tangata ʻi hono fakamaauʻi ʻoku ʻikai
ton	1 ʻOku tangilāulau ʻa Saione koeʻuhi ko hono tofiʻa kovi.
ton	12 ʻOku ne fakahā ʻene ngaahi angahala. 21 ʻOku fakamana ʻa
ton	ʻItomi. 22 ʻOku fakafiemālie ʻa Saione.
ton	‌ʻOku lelei ʻakinautolu ʻoku mate ʻo tāmateʻi ʻaki ʻae
ton	heletā, ʻiate kinautolu ʻoku mate ʻi he honge;
ton	pea ʻoku ʻikai te tau faʻa ʻalu ʻi he ngaahi hala:
ton	‌ʻOku māʻulalo ʻa homau kia ki he fakatanga:
ton	Ko e hā ʻoku ke fakangaloʻi ʻakimautolu ʻo taʻengata,
ton	Pea ʻi heʻenau ʻalu naʻaku fanongo ki he longoaʻa ʻo honau
ton	kapakau, naʻe hangē ko e ʻuʻulu ʻoe ngaahi vai lahi, hangē
ton	ko e leʻo ʻoe māfimafi, mo e ongo mai ʻae lea, mo e
ton	longoaʻa ʻo ha fuʻu tokolahi: pea ʻi heʻenau tuʻu naʻa
ton	Pea foki ki he kapatā ʻae kapakau ʻoe ngaahi meʻa moʻui,
ton	ʻaia naʻe feuutaki, mo e longoaʻa ʻoe ngaahi teka naʻe
ton	fehangai mo kinautolu, mo e ʻuʻulu ʻoe mumuhu lahi.
ton	Pea naʻe toki pehē mai ʻe ia kiate au, “Vakai, ʻe tuku
ton	ʻae meʻa kovi ʻae tangata ka te ke teuteu ʻaki hoʻo mā
ton	Pea ko kinautolu ʻoku hao ʻiate kimoutolu te nau manatu kiate
ton	au, ʻi he ngaahi puleʻanga ʻaia ʻe ʻave pōpula ki ai
ton	ʻakinautolu, ʻo kau ka fesiʻi honau loto angahala naʻe
ton	mamaʻo ʻiate au, mo honau mata naʻe sio holi pe ki honau
ton	ngaahi tamapua: pea te nau fehiʻa ʻaupito kiate kinautolu
ton	koeʻuhi ko e ngaahi kovi ʻaia kuo nau fai ʻi heʻenau ngaahi
ton	Ko ia ia te u ʻomi ai ʻae fungani kovi mei he hiteni, pea te
ton	nau maʻu honau ngaahi fale: te u ngaohi foki ke ngata ʻae
ton	fakaʻeiʻeiki ʻoe kau mālohi; pea ʻe fakaʻuliʻi ʻa honau
ton	Pea ne pehē kiate kinautolu, “Fakaʻuliʻi ʻae fale pea
ton	fakapito hono ngaahi lotoʻā ʻaki ʻae mate: mou ʻalu atu.”
ton	Pea naʻa nau ʻalu atu ʻo tāmateʻi ʻi he kolo.
ton	Pea ne toki pehē kiate au, “Foha ʻoe tangata, ko e kau
ton	tangata ʻena ʻoku fakatupu ʻae kovi, ʻonau fakakaukau kovi
ton	Te ke fua ia ʻi honau ʻao ki ho uma, pea ke fetuku atu ia ʻi
ton	he uulikelekele: te ke pūlou ho mata ke ʻoua naʻa ke sio ki
ton	he kelekele: he kuo u tuku koe ko e fakaʻilonga ki he fale ʻo
ton	‌ʻIkai kuo mou mamata ki he meʻa hā mai ʻoku vaʻinga, pea
ton	ʻikai kuo mou lea ʻaki ʻae kikite loi ʻi hoʻomou pehē,
ton	ʻOku pehē ʻe Sihova; kae ʻosi ʻoku ʻikai te u lea au?”
ton	“Foha ʻoe tangata, ʻoka angahala ʻae fonua kiate au ʻi
ton	heʻene fai kovi lahi, te u toki mafao atu ai hoku nima, pea ʻe
ton	maumau ʻae falalaʻanga ʻoe mā ʻoku ʻi ai, pea te u tuku ia
ton	ke hongea, pea motuhi mei ai ʻae tangata mo e manu:
ton	Naʻaku fakakofuʻaki koe ʻae tuitui fakasanisani, pea u
ton	fakatopuvaʻe ʻaki koe ʻae kiliʻi pasa; pea u fakavala ʻaki
ton	koe ʻae tupenu lelei, pea naʻaku ʻufiʻufi koe ʻaki ʻae
ton	Pea te nau ʻomi mo e niʻihi kiate koe, pea te nau lisingi koe
ton	ʻaki ʻae maka, pea tui ʻaki koe ʻenau heletā ke ʻasi.
ton	Pea naʻe tupu ia ʻo hoko ko e vaine pukupuku ka naʻe
ton	holoholofa ʻi lalo, pea hanga hono ngaahi vaʻa kiate ia, pea

ton	Pea kuo ʻikai fakamālohiʻi ʻe ia ha taha,
ton	pe te ne tonoʻi ʻae uaifi ʻo hono kaungāʻapi,
ton	naʻa ne tokoto hifo ʻi he lotolotonga ʻoe fanga laione,

ton	lahi ʻaupito ʻa hoku ngaahi ʻaho tapu: ko ia ne u pehē, te u
ton	lilingi hoku houhau kiate kinautolu ʻi he toafa, ke nau ʻauha

ton	faianga, ʻaia kuo mou fakalielia ai; pea te mou fehiʻa kiate
ton	kimoutolu ʻi homou ʻao pe ʻomoutolu, koeʻuhi ko e ngaahi

ton	taʻemamae ki he tokotoko?” ʻoku pehē ʻe Sihova ko e
ton	ʻOtua, “ʻe ʻikai toe ʻi ai ia.

ton	ki ho kaungāʻapi, pea kuo ke fakangalongaloʻi au,” ʻoku

ton	‌ʻIo, te ke inu ia mo mimisi ia ke maha,

ton	tangata pea mo e manu; pea te u ngaohi ia ke lala ʻo fai mei

ton	ʻe malu pe ʻenau nofo, pea ʻe ʻikai ha taha te ne faʻa

ton	‌ʻE Pelitisasa, ko e ʻeiki ʻoe kau fai meʻa mana, ʻoku ou

ton	‌ʻOua naʻa ke viki kiate au, ʻe hoku fili:
ton	ʻe tuli ʻa honau telinga.
ton	Vakai, ʻi he ngaahi moʻunga ʻae vaʻe ʻo ia ʻoku ʻomi ʻae
ton	ongoongolelei, ʻaia ʻoku fakahā ʻae melino! ʻE Siuta, tauhi
ton	ki hoʻo ngaahi kātoanga mamafa, fai hoʻo ngaahi fuakava:
ton	koeʻuhi ʻe ʻikai kei laka ʻiate koe ʻae angahala; kuo
ton	‌ʻE kai koe ʻe he afi ʻi ai; ʻe motuhi koe ʻe he heletā,

ton	ʻa Sione ki heʻene kau ākonga.”
ton	“ʻOka ʻalu ʻae laumālie ʻuli ʻi ha tangata, ʻoku ʻalu
ton	fano ia ʻi he ngaahi potu mōmoa, ʻo kumi mālōlōʻanga, kae
ton	ʻikai ʻilo ; pea pehē ʻe ia, ‘Te u toe ʻalu ki hoku fale
ton	‌ʻO nau lamasi, mo kumi ke femioʻekina ia mei hono ngutu,
ton	koeʻuhi ke nau talatalaakiʻi ia.

ton	te mou inu, pea ʻoua naʻa mou loto fakataʻetaʻetui.
ton	‌ʻOku ou tala kiate koe, ʻE ʻikai te ke ʻalu mei ai,
ton	kaeʻoua ke ke ʻatu ʻae totongi kotoa pē.”
ton	Pea te nau haʻu mei he potu hahake mo hihifo, mei he tokelau mo

ton	ʻakinautolu ke haʻu, kae fonu ai hoku fale.

ton	tamaioʻeiki totongi ʻa ʻeku tamai kuo lahi mo toe ʻenau mā,
ton	ka ʻoku ou mate ʻi he fiekaia!

ton	puli ʻiate kinautolu ʻae lea ni, ʻo ʻikai te nau ʻilo ʻae

ton	uaifi, pea mate ia taʻehaʻanefānau, ke maʻu ʻe hono tokoua
